Ragdoll stale transform contract audit

Goal:
  Existing guard covers NULL bone entries. The reported bug is stale-but-valid state:
  head/neck transform rotates around the wrong axis after save-load.
  This script maps writers/readers/destructors for ragdoll bone tables and transform fields
  so we can distinguish incomplete init, stale PDD object reuse, and block-tier buffer reuse.

======================================================================
